     5	Version: v1.0
     6	Pipeline: contract-extraction v2 with narrative pass
     7	
     8	## Project Overview
     9	
    10	ZINC-FUSION-V16 is a commodity procurement forecasting platform focused on ZL futures price-level intelligence for buy-side operations. The system combines Supabase-hosted ingestion, Next.js API and UI surfaces, and a Python forecasting pipeline. Operational safety depends on contract alignment across SQL ingest writers, API envelopes, horizon normalization, and freshness semantics presented to procurement users.
    11	
    12	This requirements set is derived from Phase 1 exploration evidence in `quality/EXPLORATION.md` and targets the highest-risk divergence vectors discovered there: telemetry contract split, architecture/gate drift, fallback-contract mismatch, envelope inconsistency, mixed-vintage miscommunication, and duplicated horizon logic.
    13	
    14	## Use Cases
    15	
    16	### UC-01: Record an ingest run lifecycle event across SQL and TS writers
    17	
    18	- Actors: pg_cron SQL functions, API helper writer.
    19	- Preconditions: An ingest job starts, succeeds, or fails.
    20	- Steps:
    21	  1. Writer allocates or receives a run identifier.
    22	  2. Writer emits start record to `ops.ingest_run`.
    23	  3. Writer updates same run record to terminal status and timestamps.
    24	- Postconditions: Telemetry rows are query-consistent across writers.
    25	- Alternative paths: On ingest failure, terminal status and error message are still written.
    26	- Requirements: REQ-001
    27	
    28	### UC-02: Verify architecture-compliant auth and gate behavior without cron-route dependency
    29	
    30	- Actors: Middleware, verification scripts.
    31	- Preconditions: Protected route request or verification run.
    32	- Steps:
    33	  1. Middleware enforces auth/session rules.
    34	  2. Verification gates evaluate architecture compliance.
    35	  3. No component assumes `/api/cron` surface exists.
    36	- Postconditions: Compliant builds are not blocked by forbidden-route checks.
    37	- Alternative paths: Gate outputs actionable architecture mismatch evidence.
    38	- Requirements: REQ-002
    39	
    40	### UC-03: Serve intraday ZL bars with deterministic fallback semantics
    41	
    42	- Actors: `/api/zl/intraday` route.
    43	- Preconditions: User requests intraday bars.
    44	- Steps:
    45	  1. Route loads primary 15m dataset.
    46	  2. If primary unavailable, route follows explicitly documented fallback behavior.
    47	  3. Response contract communicates the data-source path used.
    48	- Postconditions: Client expectations match real behavior.
    49	- Alternative paths: If no fallback exists, route and docs declare no-fallback explicitly.
    50	- Requirements: REQ-003
    51	
    52	### UC-04: Enforce consistent envelope contract across forecast and dashboard APIs
    53	
    54	- Actors: API routes, contract types, parity gate scripts.
    55	- Preconditions: Success or failure responses emitted by covered endpoints.
    56	- Steps:
    57	  1. Contract type declares required and optional fields.
    58	  2. Route handlers serialize envelopes accordingly.
    59	  3. Gate checks validate only declared requirements.
    60	- Postconditions: Parity failures indicate product defects, not harness drift.
    61	- Alternative paths: Endpoint-specific exceptions are documented and consistently enforced.
    62	- Requirements: REQ-004
    63	
    64	### UC-05: Render risk-factor freshness with transparent mixed-vintage semantics
    65	
    66	- Actors: Risk-factor API and dashboard card UI.
    67	- Preconditions: Component timestamps differ across factors.
    68	- Steps:
    69	  1. API emits min/max/as-of and mixed-vintage fields.
    70	  2. UI shows degraded-state freshness messaging.
    71	  3. Operator can distinguish globally stale from partially stale vectors.
    72	- Postconditions: Procurement timing decisions use correct recency confidence.
    73	- Alternative paths: If metadata absent, UI displays explicit unknown-freshness state.
    74	- Requirements: REQ-005
    75	
    76	### UC-06.a: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/forecast`
    77	
    78	- Actors: Forecast route.
    79	- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
    80	- Steps: Apply canonical allowlist and legacy remap.
    81	- Postconditions: Returned series uses canonical horizon set.
    82	- Requirements: REQ-006
    83	
    84	### UC-06.b: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/target-zones`
    85	
    86	- Actors: Target-zones route.
    87	- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
    88	- Steps: Apply same normalization logic as UC-06.a.
    89	- Postconditions: Target-zone horizons align with forecast horizons.
    90	- Requirements: REQ-006
    91	
    92	### UC-06.c: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/forecast-targets`
    93	
    94	- Actors: Forecast-targets route.
    95	- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
    96	- Steps: Apply same normalization logic as UC-06.a and UC-06.b.
    97	- Postconditions: Probability-surface horizons align with other forecast surfaces.
    98	- Requirements: REQ-006

   100	## Cross-Cutting Concerns
   101	
   102	- **Architecture authority:** Repository policy (`AGENTS.md`) is authoritative over historical middleware or gate assumptions.
   103	- **Telemetry integrity:** Ingest observability must stay coherent across language boundaries (SQL and TypeScript writers).
   104	- **Contract traceability:** API contract types, route payloads, and gate scripts must remain synchronized.
   105	- **Degradation transparency:** Fallback and mixed-vintage behaviors must be explicit in machine and user-facing surfaces.
   106	
   107	## Functional Sections
   108	
   109	### Ingestion Observability and Lifecycle Contracts
   110	
   111	#### REQ-001: `ops.ingest_run` writers MUST use one normalized run contract
   112	
   113	- Functional section: Ingestion Observability and Lifecycle Contracts
   114	- Tier: 3
   115	- Pattern: parity
   116	- References: `supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql:3-14`; `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:50-52`; `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:55-57`; `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4`
   117	- Linked use cases: UC-01
   118	- Requirement: Every SQL and TypeScript writer that inserts or updates `ops.ingest_run` MUST include stable `run_id` lifecycle semantics and one canonical status vocabulary.
   119	- Conditions of satisfaction:
   120	  1. `ops.ingest_run` DDL defines `run_id UUID PRIMARY KEY` and writer inserts honor that key.
   121	  2. Each writer emits start and terminal state for the same `run_id`.
   122	  3. Status values are normalized (no mixed uppercase/lowercase contract split).
   123	  4. Error paths log terminal status with timestamp and error detail.
   124	
   125	### Architecture Policy and Verification Alignment
   126	
   127	#### REQ-002: Verification and auth scaffolding MUST not require `/api/cron`
   128	
   129	- Functional section: Architecture Policy and Verification Alignment
   130	- Tier: 3
   131	- Pattern: whitelist
   132	- References: `AGENTS.md:44-45`; `AGENTS.md:149-160`; `lib/supabase/proxy.ts:15-42`; `scripts/verify/gate3.sh:5`
   133	- Linked use cases: UC-02
   134	- Requirement: Middleware and verification logic MUST treat pg_cron-only architecture as authoritative and MUST NOT enforce `/api/cron` route presence.
   135	- Conditions of satisfaction:
   136	  1. Middleware rules do not carve out `/api/cron` behavior that contradicts architecture policy.
   137	  2. Gate scripts verify policy-conformant surfaces instead of forbidden route patterns.
   138	  3. Documentation and scripts share the same architecture truth source.
   139	
   140	### Intraday Data Contract Fidelity
   141	
   142	#### REQ-003: `/api/zl/intraday` MUST align documented fallback with implementation
   143	
   144	- Functional section: Intraday Data Contract Fidelity
   145	- Tier: 3
   146	- References: `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:10-16`; `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:17-20`
   147	- Linked use cases: UC-03
   148	- Requirement: Intraday route behavior, comments, and consumer assumptions MUST agree on whether 1m fallback exists.
   149	- Conditions of satisfaction:
   150	  1. If fallback is claimed, route executes an explicit 15m→1m fallback query path.
   151	  2. If fallback is not implemented, comments and downstream expectations state that explicitly.
   152	  3. Response metadata identifies the effective data source path for debugging and parity checks.
   153	
   154	### API Envelope and Parity Contract Consistency
   155	
   156	#### REQ-004: Forecast/dashboard API surfaces, contract types, and parity harness MUST agree on envelope semantics
   157	
   158	- Functional section: API Envelope and Parity Contract Consistency
   159	- Tier: 3
   160	- Pattern: parity
   161	- References: `lib/contracts/api.ts:3-9`; `scripts/verify/gate6.sh:74-80`; `app/api/zl/live/route.ts:28-33`; `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:74-79`; `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:97-100`
   162	- Linked use cases: UC-04
   163	- Requirement: The shared envelope contract MUST define one source of truth for required vs optional fields and all covered routes/gates MUST enforce the same semantics.
   164	- Conditions of satisfaction:
   165	  1. Optional fields (for example `warning`) are optional everywhere they appear.
   166	  2. Success/failure envelope families are documented and validated consistently.
   167	  3. Endpoint-specific envelope exceptions are intentional, documented, and parity-tested.
   168	
   169	### Freshness Transparency for Procurement Decisions
   170	
   171	#### REQ-005: Risk-factor freshness MUST expose mixed-vintage state without mislabeling oldest timestamp as global freshness
   172	
   173	- Functional section: Freshness Transparency for Procurement Decisions
   174	- Tier: 3
   175	- Pattern: compensation

     1	# Quality Constitution: ZINC-FUSION-V16
     2	> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
     3	> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16
     4	
     5	## Purpose
     6	
     7	Quality for ZINC-FUSION-V16 means procurement decisions are safe to act on under real market volatility, not just that routes return HTTP 200. Data freshness, contract consistency, and horizon alignment must stay correct across ingest SQL, API handlers, and dashboard rendering.
     8	
     9	Deming applies here as an engineering workflow rule: quality is built into artifacts that every future AI or human session must inherit (`QUALITY.md`, `REQUIREMENTS.md`, protocol docs, and functional tests). Juran applies as fitness-for-use: Chris and Kevin need reliable ZL price-level intelligence to make buy/wait decisions. Crosby applies as operational cost control: one hour spent preventing silent freshness drift is cheaper than a week of bad procurement timing.
    10	
    11	## Coverage Targets
    12	
    13	| Subsystem | Target | Why |
    14	|---|---:|---|
    15	| `ops.ingest_run` cross-writer contract | 95% | Inconsistent run telemetry can hide ingest failure and break incident response. |
    16	| Auth and verification gate policy | 90% | `/api/cron` assumptions can reintroduce forbidden architecture or block compliant releases. |
    17	| ZL API envelope family | 90% | Divergent envelope semantics create false parity failures and brittle client behavior. |
    18	| Risk-factor freshness and mixed-vintage signaling | 92% | Stale freshness presentation can mislead procurement timing. |
    19	| Forecast horizon normalization | 95% | Horizon drift across forecast surfaces breaks chart/target/probability parity. |
    20	| AI snapshot ingest and fallback signaling | 90% | Silent snapshot rejection degrades AI-first cards without operator visibility. |
    21	| Pipeline readiness signaling | 85% | Scaffold phases in `--all` runs can overstate production readiness. |
    22	
    23	## Coverage Theater Prevention
    24	
    25	- Passing tests that only assert `ok: true` without validating envelope shape.
    26	- Testing fallback code by asserting output exists, but not asserting downgrade indicators.
    27	- Source-inspection tests that never run (`run=False`, disabled guards left in place forever).
    28	- Tests that verify only one forecast endpoint while claiming horizon consistency for three endpoints.
    29	- Mock-only ingest tests that never verify shared table contract fields (`run_id`, status vocabulary).
    30	- Gate scripts that check legacy route shapes (`/api/cron`) instead of architecture policy.
    31	- Freshness tests that verify one date field but ignore mixed-vintage semantics.
    32	
    33	## Fitness-to-Purpose Scenarios
    34	
    35	### Scenario 1: Ingest Telemetry Contract Split
    36	
    37	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-001]
    38	
    39	**What happened:** `ops.ingest_run` requires `run_id`, but legacy SQL writers insert rows without it while TS helpers write uppercase status enums. This permits partial observability and fragmented status semantics across the same table.
    40	
    41	**The requirement:** All ingest writers must use one lifecycle contract: explicit `run_id`, canonical status vocabulary, and deterministic start/success/failure transitions.
    42	
    43	**How to verify:** `test_req001_all_ingest_writers_include_run_id_and_canonical_status` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    44	
    45	### Scenario 2: Forbidden Cron Surface Drift
    46	
    47	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-002]
    48	
    49	**What happened:** Architecture policy forbids Vercel cron routes, but middleware and verification logic still encode `/api/cron` assumptions. This can block compliant builds or push engineers toward forbidden route resurrection.
    50	
    51	**The requirement:** Auth middleware and verification gates must validate pg_cron-only architecture without requiring `/api/cron` endpoints.
    52	
    53	**How to verify:** `test_req002_no_runtime_or_gate_dependency_on_api_cron_path` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    54	
    55	### Scenario 3: Intraday Fallback Promise Divergence
    56	
    57	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-003]
    58	
    59	**What happened:** `/api/zl/intraday` claims a 15m→1m fallback in comments while querying only `mkt.price_15m`. Consumers can trust resilience that is not implemented.
    60	
    61	**The requirement:** Either implement fallback behavior to `mkt.price_1m` or remove fallback claims and align client assumptions.
    62	
    63	**How to verify:** `test_req003_intraday_route_contract_matches_implemented_fallback` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    64	
    65	### Scenario 4: Envelope Contract Drift Across Surfaces
    66	
    67	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-004]
    68	
    69	**What happened:** Route responses, shared API contract types, and parity gate checks disagree about optional vs required envelope fields (`warning`, shape differences). False-negative parity failures can mask real regressions.
    70	
    71	**The requirement:** Contract types, route envelopes, and verification scripts must share one consistent envelope policy.
    72	
    73	**How to verify:** `test_req004_contract_and_gate_align_on_warning_semantics` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    74	
    75	### Scenario 5: Mixed-Vintage Freshness Misread
    76	
    77	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-005]
    78	
    79	**What happened:** Risk-factor API sets canonical `as_of_date` to oldest component date while also exposing min/max range. Dashboard messaging can be interpreted as fully stale even when only part of vector is stale.
    80	
    81	**The requirement:** Mixed-vintage data must be explicitly signaled as degraded with field-level transparency.
    82	
    83	**How to verify:** `test_req005_risk_factor_payload_exposes_mixed_vintage_metadata` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    84	
    85	### Scenario 6: Forecast Horizon Normalization Drift
    86	
    87	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-006]
    88	
    89	**What happened:** `normalizeHorizon` logic is duplicated across three endpoints. A one-file edit can desynchronize forecast, target-zone, and probability surfaces.
    90	
    91	**The requirement:** Horizon normalization constants and mapping behavior must remain equivalent across all forecast-facing endpoints.
    92	
    93	**How to verify:** `test_req006_normalize_horizon_logic_is_identical_across_three_routes` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    94	
    95	### Scenario 7: Snapshot Source Whitelist Regression
    96	
    97	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-004]
    98	
    99	**What happened:** Snapshot source labels are hard-whitelisted. A source-label drift can silently null out snapshots and trigger unannounced fallback narratives.
   100	
   101	**The requirement:** Whitelist changes must be deliberate, and fallback behavior must expose reliability downgrade cues.
   102	
   103	**How to verify:** `test_scenario_snapshot_source_whitelist_is_explicit_and_auditable` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
   104	
   105	### Scenario 8: Scaffold Pipeline Misreported as Ready
   106	
   107	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-001]
   108	
   109	**What happened:** `pipeline.py --all` includes scaffold phases returning `status: scaffold`. Operators can read full-run completion as inference readiness.
   110	
   111	**The requirement:** Scaffold status must remain explicit and blocked from “ready” interpretation until implemented.
   112	
   113	**How to verify:** `test_scenario_pipeline_order_and_scaffold_modules_are_visible` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
   114	
   115	## AI Session Quality Discipline
   116	
   117	1. Read `quality/QUALITY.md` and `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md` before changing behavior.
   118	2. Preserve every REQ `Pattern` tag in both Markdown and manifest outputs.
   119	3. Treat cross-file consistency requirements as first-class; do not verify routes in isolation.
   120	4. Run mechanical enumeration verification before asserting completeness claims.
   121	5. Never classify a payload as fresh without validating mixed-vintage metadata fields.
   122	6. Do not close a quality phase until artifacts, manifests, and receipts are all on disk.
   123	
   124	## The Human Gate
   125	
   126	- Procurement risk appetite decisions for stale or mixed-vintage data tolerance.
   127	- Final severity of architecture-policy drift findings that affect release timelines.
   128	- Decisions to standardize envelope shape vs retaining backward-compatible variants.
   129	- Approval to change ingest status vocabulary in production tables.
   130	- Go/no-go on interpreting scaffold pipeline phases as launch-ready.

    29	
    30	## 1. Principles
    31	
    32	### What V16 Is
    33	
    34	- A from-scratch rebuild — **no code transferred from legacy baseline**
    35	- legacy baseline stays live as reference and rollback during the entire build
    36	- legacy baseline is a reference for _what the product does_, not a source of code to port
    37	- Purpose: eliminate all drift, errors, mismatches, legacy baggage, Inngest complexity
    38	
    39	### What V16 Is Not
    40	
    41	- Not a migration-in-place
    42	- Not a refactor of legacy baseline
    43	- Not a copy-paste with cleanup
    44	- Not allowed to inherit: the old Prisma migration chain, copied `.vercel/` state, hand-copied `.env.local` habits, the Inngest estate, dead pages, dead jobs, or unclear contracts
    45	
    46	### Non-Negotiable Rules
    47	
    48	1. No old migration history crosses the boundary
    49	2. Every table must have a reader AND a writer
    50	3. Every page must justify its data dependencies
    51	4. Every job must justify its existence
    52	5. Start from the screen, not the schema
    53	6. Rewrite the chart from scratch using legacy baseline as visual reference — settings were hard-won, preserve behavior exactly
    54	7. Rewrite the landing page from scratch using legacy baseline as visual reference — specific and intentional design to preserve
    55	8. ProFarmer is mandatory ($500/month)
    56	9. 11 specialists — never 10. `trump_effect` is the 11th.
    57	10. Target = future price level. Target Zones = horizontal lines. Never cones, bands, or funnels.
    58	
    59	---

    70	| **Both**                                                                    | Policy/legislation impact on soy oil                 | Legislation page                                  |
    71	| **Both**                                                                    | Market sentiment read                                | Sentiment page                                    |

   109	- Over-normalized Vegas tables (17 → 7)

   113	
   114	## 3. Target Architecture
   115	
   116	### Stack
   117	
   118	| Layer                  | legacy baseline (current)       | V16 (target)                                                       |
   119	| ---------------------- | ------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------ |
   120	| **Database**           | Prisma Postgres (cloud)         | Supabase Postgres                                                  |
   121	| **Schema mgmt**        | Prisma + 34 migrations          | Supabase migrations (SQL-first)                                    |
   122	| **Frontend**           | Next.js on Vercel               | Next.js on Vercel (new project) + shadcn/ui + Radix + Tailwind CSS |
   123	| **Scheduling**         | Inngest (104 functions)         | pg_cron + http extension (all ingestion inside Postgres)           |
   124	| **DB client (TS)**     | pg.Pool + Prisma for validation | Supabase JS client + pg.Pool for bulk                              |
   125	| **DB client (Python)** | psycopg2 direct                 | psycopg2 direct to Supabase Postgres                               |
   126	| **ML**                 | AutoGluon (local, CPU)          | AutoGluon (local, CPU) — rebuilt clean                             |
   127	| **Specialists**        | 11 Python signal generators     | 11 Python signal generators — rebuilt clean                        |
   128	| **Auth**               | Custom cookie-based             | Supabase Auth                                                      |
   129	| **Env mgmt**           | Manual .env.local               | Vercel <> Supabase integration, `vercel env pull`                  |
   130	| **API secrets**        | Manual env vars                 | Supabase Vault (`current_setting()`)                               |
   131	| **UI system**          | Mixed CSS + shadcn/ui           | shadcn/ui + Radix + Tailwind CSS + ZINC Fusion brand tokens        |
   132	
   133	### Cloud Supabase ONLY — No Local Supabase
   134	
   135	| Scenario                      | Approach                                                                                                                                                  | Why                                                                                                                                                   |
   136	| ----------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
   137	| **Frontend dev**              | Reads from cloud Supabase                                                                                                                                 | Single source of truth. No local/cloud drift. `vercel env pull` provides connection.                                                                  |
   138	| **Python training/inference** | Reads canonical raw data from cloud Supabase, can materialize the bounded AG training source into local PostgreSQL for training, and writes intermediates to **local parquet files** during compute. Promotes validated outputs back to cloud. | Cloud is canonical. Local PostgreSQL is a training-source staging database only, not Supabase and not serving truth. Intermediates stay local during iteration. Only validated artifacts are promoted back to cloud DB. |
   139	| **Data ingestion**            | Runs **INSIDE Postgres** via pg_cron + http extension                                                                                                     | No Vercel cron routes. No external orchestrator. Ingestion is a database-native operation.                                                            |
   140	| **Supabase CLI**              | Used for migrations ONLY (`supabase db push`, `supabase db diff --linked`)                                                                                | No `supabase status`. No `supabase start`. No local Supabase runtime. Local PostgreSQL, when used, is a separate AG training-source database. |
   141	
   142	**Guard rail:** Create a `training` Postgres role that can only write to `training.*` and `forecasts.*` schemas. The Python pipeline uses this role. Frontend service role is read-only on those schemas.
   143	
   144	### Architecture Diagram
   145	
   146	```
   147	+-----------------------------------------------------------+
   148	|                      BROWSER                               |
   149	|  Next.js App (Vercel) -- 6 pages                          |
   150	|  Supabase JS client for auth + reads                      |
   151	+---------------------------+-------------------------------+
   152	                            |
   153	+---------------------------v-------------------------------+
   154	|                       VERCEL                               |
   155	|  Frontend hosting ONLY + read-only API routes              |
   156	|  No cron routes. No data ingestion.                        |
   157	|  Env: auto-injected via Supabase integration               |
   158	+---------------------------+-------------------------------+
   159	                            |
   160	+---------------------------v-------------------------------+
   161	|                      SUPABASE                              |
   162	|  Single cloud DB (9 schemas: mkt, econ, alt, supply,      |
   163	|    training, forecasts, analytics, ops, vegas)              |
   164	|  pg_cron + http extension (ALL data ingestion ~22 jobs)    |
   165	|  Vault (API keys via current_setting())                    |
   166	|  Auth (user authentication)                                |
   167	|  RLS policies per schema                                   |
   168	+-----------------------------------------------------------+
   169	
   170	+-----------------------------------------------------------+
   171	|              LOCAL MACHINE (compute workspace)              |
   172	|  Python ML Pipeline (rebuilt from scratch)                  |
   173	|  - Reads raw data from cloud Supabase via psycopg2         |
   174	|    (cloud is canonical; local PostgreSQL is AG staging only) |
   175	|  - Writes intermediates to local parquet files              |
   176	|  - promote_to_cloud.py pushes validated outputs to cloud   |
   177	|                                                            |
   178	|  ProFarmer Scraper (Python Playwright, system cron)        |
   179	|  - Writes directly to cloud Supabase                       |
   180	+-----------------------------------------------------------+

     1	import type { SupabaseClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
     2	
     3	export type IngestRunStatus = "RUNNING" | "SUCCESS" | "FAILED";
     4	
     5	export async function logIngestRunStart(
     6	  client: SupabaseClient,
     7	  jobName: string,
     8	  source: string,
     9	): Promise<string> {
    10	  const runId = crypto.randomUUID();
    11	
    12	  try {
    13	    await client.schema("ops").from("ingest_run").insert({
    14	      run_id: runId,
    15	      job_name: jobName,
    16	      source,
    17	      status: "RUNNING",
    18	      started_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    19	      records_upserted: 0,
    20	    });
    21	  } catch (error) {
    22	    console.error("Failed to write ops.ingest_run start record", error);
    23	  }
    24	
    25	  return runId;
    26	}
    27	
    28	export async function logIngestRunFinish(
    29	  client: SupabaseClient,
    30	  runId: string,
    31	  recordsUpserted: number,
    32	): Promise<void> {
    33	  try {
    34	    await client
    35	      .schema("ops")
    36	      .from("ingest_run")
    37	      .update({
    38	        status: "SUCCESS",
    39	        finished_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    40	        records_upserted: recordsUpserted,
    41	      })
    42	      .eq("run_id", runId);
    43	  } catch (error) {
    44	    console.error("Failed to write ops.ingest_run success record", error);
    45	  }
    46	}
    47	
    48	export async function logIngestRunFailure(
    49	  client: SupabaseClient,
    50	  runId: string,
    51	  errorMessage: string,
    52	): Promise<void> {
    53	  try {
    54	    await client
    55	      .schema("ops")
    56	      .from("ingest_run")
    57	      .update({
    58	        status: "FAILED",
    59	        finished_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    60	        error_message: errorMessage.slice(0, 2000),
    61	      })
    62	      .eq("run_id", runId);
    63	  } catch (error) {
    64	    console.error("Failed to write ops.ingest_run failure record", error);
    65	  }
    66	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	-- =============================================================================
     2	-- ingest_zl_intraday() + rollup_zl_daily()
     3	--
     4	-- Pulls 1h ZL bars from Databento REST API into mkt.price_1h.
     5	-- Rolls up 1h bars into mkt.price_1d daily bars.
     6	-- Updates mkt.latest_price with the most recent close.
     7	-- Logs all runs to ops.ingest_run.
     8	--
     9	-- pg_cron: runs hourly. 1h bars form the daily bar progressively.
    10	-- =============================================================================
    11	
    12	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    13	-- Function A: ingest_zl_intraday()
    14	--
    15	-- Fetches 1h OHLCV bars from Databento for ZL continuous front-month.
    16	-- Uses the newest bar in mkt.price_1h to determine the start date.
    17	-- Databento returns NDJSON (newline-delimited JSON lines).
    18	-- Prices are fixed-point integers (divide by 1e9).
    19	-- ts_event is nanosecond epoch.
    20	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    21	CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION ingest_zl_intraday()
    22	RETURNS jsonb
    23	SECURITY DEFINER
    24	SET search_path = public, extensions
    25	LANGUAGE plpgsql
    26	AS $$
    27	DECLARE
    28	  api_key     TEXT;
    29	  start_date  TEXT;
    30	  end_date    TEXT;
    31	  url         TEXT;
    32	  response    http_response;
    33	  line        TEXT;
    34	  rec         JSONB;
    35	  bar_ts      TIMESTAMPTZ;
    36	  bar_open    NUMERIC;
    37	  bar_high    NUMERIC;
    38	  bar_low     NUMERIC;
    39	  bar_close   NUMERIC;
    40	  bar_volume  BIGINT;
    41	  records_in  INT := 0;
    42	  started     TIMESTAMPTZ := now();
    43	BEGIN
    44	  -- 1. Get API key from Vault
    45	  SELECT decrypted_secret INTO api_key
    46	  FROM vault.decrypted_secrets
    47	  WHERE name = 'databento_api_key_v2';
    48	
    49	  IF api_key IS NULL THEN
    50	    INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
    51	    VALUES ('ingest_zl_intraday', 'databento', started, now(), 'failed', 0, 'Databento API key not found in Vault');
    52	    RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'error', 'message', 'API key not in Vault');
    53	  END IF;
    54	
    55	  -- 2. Determine date range: start from max existing 1h bar or 30 days back
    56	  SELECT COALESCE(
    57	    to_char((max(bucket_ts) AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD'),
    58	    to_char((now() - interval '30 days')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD')
    59	  ) INTO start_date
    60	  FROM mkt.price_1h
    61	  WHERE symbol = 'ZL';
    62	
    63	  -- End = today (Databento will clamp to available data)
    64	  end_date := to_char((now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    65	
    66	  -- If start = end, go back 1 day to ensure we get today's bars
    67	  IF start_date = end_date THEN
    68	    start_date := to_char(((now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC') - interval '1 day')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    69	  END IF;
    70	
    71	  -- 3. Call Databento REST API
    72	  url := 'https://hist.databento.com/v0/timeseries.get_range'
    73	    || '?dataset=GLBX.MDP3'
    74	    || '&symbols=ZL.c.0'
    75	    || '&schema=ohlcv-1h'
    76	    || '&stype_in=continuous'
    77	    || '&start=' || start_date
    78	    || '&end=' || end_date
    79	    || '&encoding=json';
    80	
    81	  SELECT * INTO response FROM http((
    82	    'GET',
    83	    url,
    84	    ARRAY[http_header('Authorization', 'Basic ' || encode(convert_to(api_key || ':', 'UTF8'), 'base64'))],
    85	    NULL,
    86	    NULL
    87	  )::http_request);
    88	
    89	  IF response.status != 200 THEN
    90	    INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
    91	    VALUES ('ingest_zl_intraday', 'databento', started, now(), 'failed', 0,
    92	            'Databento HTTP ' || response.status || ': ' || left(response.content, 200));
    93	    RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'error', 'http_status', response.status);
    94	  END IF;
    95	
    96	  -- 4. Parse NDJSON response (one JSON object per line)
    97	  FOR line IN SELECT unnest(string_to_array(response.content, E'\n'))
    98	  LOOP
    99	    -- Skip empty lines
   100	    CONTINUE WHEN trim(line) = '';
   101	
   102	    BEGIN
   103	      rec := line::jsonb;
   104	
   105	      -- ts_event is nanosecond epoch -> convert to timestamptz
   106	      bar_ts := to_timestamp(((rec->'hd'->>'ts_event')::bigint) / 1000000000.0);
   107	
   108	      -- Prices are fixed-point (divide by 1e9)
   109	      bar_open   := (rec->>'open')::bigint   / 1000000000.0;
   110	      bar_high   := (rec->>'high')::bigint   / 1000000000.0;
   111	      bar_low    := (rec->>'low')::bigint    / 1000000000.0;
   112	      bar_close  := (rec->>'close')::bigint  / 1000000000.0;
   113	      bar_volume := (rec->>'volume')::bigint;
   114	
   115	      -- Skip bars with zero or null close
   116	      CONTINUE WHEN bar_close IS NULL OR bar_close = 0;
   117	
   118	      -- UPSERT into mkt.price_1h
   119	      INSERT INTO mkt.price_1h (symbol, bucket_ts, open, high, low, close, volume)
   120	      VALUES ('ZL', bar_ts, bar_open, bar_high, bar_low, bar_close, bar_volume)
   121	      ON CONFLICT (symbol, bucket_ts) DO UPDATE SET
   122	        open       = EXCLUDED.open,
   123	        high       = EXCLUDED.high,
   124	        low        = EXCLUDED.low,
   125	        close      = EXCLUDED.close,
   126	        volume     = EXCLUDED.volume,
   127	        ingested_at = now();
   128	
   129	      records_in := records_in + 1;
   130	
   131	    EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
   132	      -- Skip malformed lines, continue processing
   133	      CONTINUE;
   134	    END;
   135	  END LOOP;
   136	
   137	  -- 5. Log success
   138	  INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
   139	  VALUES ('ingest_zl_intraday', 'databento', started, now(), 'ok', records_in, NULL);
   140	
   141	  RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'ok', 'records', records_in, 'start', start_date, 'end', end_date);
   142	END;
   143	$$;
   144	
   145	
   146	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   147	-- Function B: rollup_zl_daily()
   148	--
   149	-- Aggregates 1h bars from mkt.price_1h into mkt.price_1d.
   150	-- For each calendar day with 1h bars:
   151	--   open  = open of first 1h bar (by bucket_ts)
   152	--   high  = max high across all 1h bars
   153	--   low   = min low across all 1h bars
   154	--   close = close of last 1h bar (by bucket_ts)
   155	--   volume = sum of all 1h bar volumes
   156	--
   157	-- Also updates mkt.latest_price with the most recent close.
   158	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   159	CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION rollup_zl_daily()
   160	RETURNS jsonb
   161	SECURITY DEFINER
   162	SET search_path = public
   163	LANGUAGE plpgsql
   164	AS $$
   165	DECLARE
   166	  records_out INT := 0;
   167	  started     TIMESTAMPTZ := now();
   168	  latest_close NUMERIC;
   169	  latest_ts    TIMESTAMPTZ;
   170	BEGIN
   171	  -- 1. Aggregate 1h bars into daily bars
   172	  --    Only process days that have 1h bars newer than the latest ingested_at in price_1d,
   173	  --    OR days that don't exist in price_1d yet.
   174	  INSERT INTO mkt.price_1d (symbol, bucket_ts, open, high, low, close, volume)
   175	  SELECT
   176	    'ZL' AS symbol,
   177	    date_trunc('day', bucket_ts AT TIME ZONE 'UTC') AS day_ts,
   178	    (ARRAY_AGG(open ORDER BY bucket_ts ASC))[1]  AS open,
   179	    MAX(high)                                      AS high,
   180	    MIN(low)                                       AS low,
   181	    (ARRAY_AGG(close ORDER BY bucket_ts DESC))[1] AS close,
   182	    SUM(volume)                                    AS volume
   183	  FROM mkt.price_1h
   184	  WHERE symbol = 'ZL'
   185	    AND bucket_ts >= COALESCE(
   186	      (SELECT max(bucket_ts) - interval '2 days' FROM mkt.price_1d WHERE symbol = 'ZL'),
   187	      '2020-01-01'::timestamptz
   188	    )
   189	  GROUP BY date_trunc('day', bucket_ts AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')
   190	  HAVING SUM(volume) >= 100  -- skip roll artifact days (< 100 total contracts)
   191	  ON CONFLICT (symbol, bucket_ts) DO UPDATE SET
   192	    open       = EXCLUDED.open,
   193	    high       = EXCLUDED.high,
   194	    low        = EXCLUDED.low,
   195	    close      = EXCLUDED.close,
   196	    volume     = EXCLUDED.volume,
   197	    ingested_at = now();
   198	
   199	  GET DIAGNOSTICS records_out = ROW_COUNT;
   200	
   201	  -- 2. Update latest_price with most recent close
   202	  SELECT close, bucket_ts INTO latest_close, latest_ts
   203	  FROM mkt.price_1d
   204	  WHERE symbol = 'ZL'
   205	  ORDER BY bucket_ts DESC
   206	  LIMIT 1;
   207	
   208	  IF latest_close IS NOT NULL THEN
   209	    INSERT INTO mkt.latest_price (symbol, price, observed_at, ingested_at)
   210	    VALUES ('ZL', latest_close, latest_ts, now())
   211	    ON CONFLICT (symbol) DO UPDATE SET
   212	      price       = EXCLUDED.price,
   213	      observed_at = EXCLUDED.observed_at,
   214	      ingested_at = now();
   215	  END IF;
   216	
   217	  -- 3. Log success
   218	  INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
   219	  VALUES ('rollup_zl_daily', 'rollup', started, now(), 'ok', records_out, NULL);
   220	
   221	  RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'ok', 'daily_bars_upserted', records_out, 'latest_price', latest_close);
   222	END;
   223	$$;
   224	
   225	
   226	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   227	-- pg_cron schedules: hourly, staggered off :00
   228	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   229	SELECT cron.schedule('ingest_zl_intraday', '7 * * * *', $$SELECT ingest_zl_intraday()$$);
   230	SELECT cron.schedule('rollup_zl_daily',    '9 * * * *', $$SELECT rollup_zl_daily()$$);

     1	-- Supabase-only trusted dashboard fill:

     5	CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill()
     6	RETURNS jsonb
     7	SECURITY DEFINER
     8	SET search_path = public, extensions
     9	LANGUAGE plpgsql
    10	AS $$
    11	DECLARE

    13	  started TIMESTAMPTZ := now();

    16	  prev_date DATE;
    17	
    18	  resp_cl http_response;
    19	  resp_cny http_response;
    20	  resp_vix http_response;

    22

    33	  uncertainty_value NUMERIC;

    38

    49	  regime TEXT;
    50	  regime_confidence NUMERIC;
    51	  v_records_upserted INT := 0;
    52	  non_null_points INT := 0;
    53	  payload JSONB;
    54	BEGIN
    55	  INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (run_id, job_name, source, status, started_at)
    56	  VALUES (v_run_id, 'trusted_site_fill', 'supabase-http-yahoo', 'running', started);
    57	
    58	  -- Avoid transient HTTP timeout failures in pgsql-http.
    59	  PERFORM extensions.http_set_curlopt('CURLOPT_CONNECTTIMEOUT_MS', '5000');
    60	  PERFORM extensions.http_set_curlopt('CURLOPT_TIMEOUT_MS', '20000');
    61	
    62	  SELECT max(trade_date) INTO prev_date
    63	  FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    64	  WHERE trade_date <= v_trade_date;
    65	
    66	  IF prev_date IS NOT NULL THEN
    67	    SELECT metric_value INTO board_crush_value
    68	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    69	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'board_crush_value'
    70	    LIMIT 1;
    71	
    72	    SELECT metric_value INTO oil_share_value
    73	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    74	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'oil_share_value'
    75	    LIMIT 1;
    76	
    77	    SELECT metric_value INTO oil_share_5d_change
    78	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    79	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'oil_share_5d_change'
    80	    LIMIT 1;
    81	
    82	    SELECT metric_value INTO uncertainty_value
    83	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    84	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'uncertainty_value'
    85	    LIMIT 1;
    86	
    87	    SELECT metric_value INTO soy_china_news_count
    88	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    89	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'soy_china_news_count'
    90	    LIMIT 1;
    91	
    92	    SELECT metric_value INTO soy_tariff_news_count
    93	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    94	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'soy_tariff_news_count'
    95	    LIMIT 1;
    96	
    97	    SELECT metric_value INTO macro_news_count
    98	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    99	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'macro_news_count'
   100	    LIMIT 1;
   101	
   102	    SELECT metric_value INTO energy_news_count
   103	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   104	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'energy_news_count'
   105	    LIMIT 1;
   106	  END IF;
   107	
   108	  SELECT * INTO resp_cl
   109	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/CL%3DF?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   110	  IF resp_cl.status = 200 THEN
   111	    WITH closes AS (
   112	      SELECT ordinality AS idx, value::text::numeric AS close
   113	      FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   114	        COALESCE(resp_cl.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   115	      ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   116	      WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   117	    ),
   118	    latest AS (
   119	      SELECT idx, close FROM closes ORDER BY idx DESC LIMIT 1
   120	    ),
   121	    anchor AS (
   122	      SELECT close FROM closes WHERE idx <= (SELECT idx FROM latest) - 5 ORDER BY idx DESC LIMIT 1
   123	    )
   124	    SELECT l.close, a.close
   125	      INTO cl_price, cl_anchor
   126	    FROM latest l
   127	    LEFT JOIN anchor a ON TRUE;
   128	  END IF;
   129	  IF cl_anchor IS NOT NULL AND cl_anchor <> 0 THEN
   130	    cl_change_5d := (cl_price - cl_anchor) / cl_anchor;
   131	  END IF;
   132	
   133	  SELECT * INTO resp_cny
   134	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/CNY%3DX?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   135	  IF resp_cny.status = 200 THEN
   136	    SELECT value::text::numeric INTO cny_rate
   137	    FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   138	      COALESCE(resp_cny.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   139	    ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   140	    WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   141	    ORDER BY ordinality DESC
   142	    LIMIT 1;
   143	  END IF;
   144	
   145	  SELECT * INTO resp_vix
   146	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/%5EVIX?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   147	  IF resp_vix.status = 200 THEN
   148	    SELECT value::text::numeric INTO vix_value
   149	    FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   150	      COALESCE(resp_vix.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   151	    ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   152	    WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   153	    ORDER BY ordinality DESC
   154	    LIMIT 1;
   155	  END IF;
   156	
   157	  SELECT * INTO resp_ovx
   158	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/%5EOVX?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   159	  IF resp_ovx.status = 200 THEN
   160	    SELECT value::text::numeric INTO ovx_value
   161	    FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   162	      COALESCE(resp_ovx.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   163	    ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   164	    WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   165	    ORDER BY ordinality DESC
   166	    LIMIT 1;
   167	  END IF;
   168	
   169	  -- If live pulls fail, keep last known values so the surface does not hard-break.
   170	  IF cl_price IS NULL THEN
   171	    SELECT metric_value INTO cl_price
   172	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   173	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'cl_price'
   174	    LIMIT 1;
   175	  END IF;
   176	  IF cl_change_5d IS NULL THEN
   177	    SELECT metric_value INTO cl_change_5d
   178	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   179	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'cl_change_5d'
   180	    LIMIT 1;
   181	  END IF;
   182	  IF cny_rate IS NULL THEN
   183	    SELECT metric_value INTO cny_rate
   184	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   185	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'cny_rate'
   186	    LIMIT 1;
   187	  END IF;
   188	  IF vix_value IS NULL THEN
   189	    SELECT metric_value INTO vix_value
   190	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   191	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'vix_value'
   192	    LIMIT 1;
   193	  END IF;
   194	  IF ovx_value IS NULL THEN
   195	    SELECT metric_value INTO ovx_value
   196	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   197	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'ovx_value'
   198	    LIMIT 1;
   199	  END IF;
   200	
   201	  soy_china_news_count := COALESCE(soy_china_news_count, 0);
   202	  soy_tariff_news_count := COALESCE(soy_tariff_news_count, 0);
   203	  macro_news_count := COALESCE(macro_news_count, 0);
   204	  energy_news_count := COALESCE(energy_news_count, 0);
   205	
   206	  vix_stress_score := round((
   207	    (CASE WHEN vix_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((vix_value - 14) / 21) * 100)) END) * 0.60 +
   208	    (CASE WHEN ovx_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((ovx_value - 25) / 55) * 100)) END) * 0.40
   209	  )::numeric, 1);
   210	
   211	  crush_pressure_score := round((
   212	    (CASE WHEN board_crush_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, (((4.2 - board_crush_value) - 0.0) / 3.5) * 100)) END) * 0.70 +
   213	    (CASE WHEN oil_share_5d_change IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((abs(oil_share_5d_change) - 0.2) / 3.8) * 100)) END) * 0.30
   214	  )::numeric, 1);
   215	
   216	  china_tension_score := round((
   217	    (CASE WHEN cny_rate IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((abs(cny_rate - 7.0) - 0.02) / 0.33) * 100)) END) * 0.70 +
   218	    (GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((soy_china_news_count - 2) / 28) * 100))) * 0.30
   219	  )::numeric, 1);
   220	
   221	  tariff_threat_score := round((
   222	    (CASE WHEN uncertainty_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((uncertainty_value - 150) / 400) * 100)) END) * 0.70 +
   223	    (GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, (((soy_tariff_news_count + macro_news_count) - 4) / 36) * 100))) * 0.30
   224	  )::numeric, 1);
   225	
   226	  energy_stress_score := round((
   227	    (CASE WHEN cl_change_5d IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, (((abs(cl_change_5d * 100)) - 0.8) / 9.2) * 100)) END) * 0.55 +
   228	    (CASE WHEN ovx_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((ovx_value - 25) / 55) * 100)) END) * 0.30 +
   229	    (GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((energy_news_count - 2) / 28) * 100))) * 0.15
   230	  )::numeric, 1);
   231	
   232	  avg_score := round(((vix_stress_score + crush_pressure_score + china_tension_score + tariff_threat_score + energy_stress_score) / 5.0)::numeric, 1);
   233	
   234	  top_driver_key := 'vix_stress';
   235	  top_driver_score := vix_stress_score;
   236	  IF crush_pressure_score > top_driver_score THEN
   237	    top_driver_key := 'crush_pressure';
   238	    top_driver_score := crush_pressure_score;
   239	  END IF;
   240	  IF china_tension_score > top_driver_score THEN
   241	    top_driver_key := 'china_tension';
   242	    top_driver_score := china_tension_score;
   243	  END IF;
   244	  IF tariff_threat_score > top_driver_score THEN
   245	    top_driver_key := 'tariff_threat';
   246	    top_driver_score := tariff_threat_score;
   247	  END IF;
   248	  IF energy_stress_score > top_driver_score THEN
   249	    top_driver_key := 'energy_stress';
   250	    top_driver_score := energy_stress_score;
   251	  END IF;
   252	
   253	  IF avg_score >= 78 AND top_driver_score >= 85 THEN
   254	    posture := 'DEFER';
   255	  ELSIF avg_score >= 62 THEN
   256	    posture := 'WAIT';
   257	  ELSE
   258	    posture := 'ACCUMULATE';
   259	  END IF;
   260	
   261	  IF avg_score >= 70 THEN
   262	    regime := 'SUPPLY_CRISIS';
   263	  ELSIF avg_score >= 55 THEN
   264	    regime := 'BEARISH';
   265	  ELSIF avg_score <= 30 THEN
   266	    regime := 'BULLISH';
   267	  ELSE
   268	    regime := 'NEUTRAL';
   269	  END IF;
   270	
   271	  non_null_points :=
   272	    (CASE WHEN cl_price IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   273	    (CASE WHEN cl_change_5d IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   274	    (CASE WHEN cny_rate IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   275	    (CASE WHEN vix_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   276	    (CASE WHEN ovx_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   277	    (CASE WHEN board_crush_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   278	    (CASE WHEN oil_share_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   279	    (CASE WHEN oil_share_5d_change IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   280	    (CASE WHEN uncertainty_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END);
   281	  regime_confidence := round(LEAST(0.95, 0.45 + non_null_points * 0.05)::numeric, 4);
   282	
   283	  payload := jsonb_build_object(
   284	    'source', 'supabase_pg_cron_trusted_fill',
   285	    'asOf', now_et_iso,
   286	    'carriedFromDate', prev_date,
   287	    'pulledBy', 'ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill'
   288	  );
   289	
   290	  INSERT INTO analytics.dashboard_metrics (trade_date, metric_key, metric_value, payload)
   291	  VALUES
   292	    (v_trade_date, 'vix_value', vix_value, payload),
   293	    (v_trade_date, 'ovx_value', ovx_value, payload),
   294	    (v_trade_date, 'cl_price', cl_price, payload),
   295	    (v_trade_date, 'cl_change_5d', cl_change_5d, payload),
   296	    (v_trade_date, 'oil_change_5d', cl_change_5d, payload),
   297	    (v_trade_date, 'cny_rate', cny_rate, payload),
   298	    (v_trade_date, 'board_crush_value', board_crush_value, payload),
   299	    (v_trade_date, 'oil_share_value', oil_share_value, payload),
   300	    (v_trade_date, 'oil_share_5d_change', oil_share_5d_change, payload),
   301	    (v_trade_date, 'uncertainty_value', uncertainty_value, payload),
   302	    (v_trade_date, 'tpu_value', uncertainty_value, payload),
   303	    (v_trade_date, 'soy_china_news_count', soy_china_news_count, payload),
   304	    (v_trade_date, 'soy_tariff_news_count', soy_tariff_news_count, payload),
   305	    (v_trade_date, 'macro_news_count', macro_news_count, payload),
   306	    (v_trade_date, 'energy_news_count', energy_news_count, payload),
   307	    (v_trade_date, 'vix_stress_score', vix_stress_score, payload),
   308	    (v_trade_date, 'crush_pressure_score', crush_pressure_score, payload),
   309	    (v_trade_date, 'china_tension_score', china_tension_score, payload),
   310	    (v_trade_date, 'tariff_threat_score', tariff_threat_score, payload),
   311	    (v_trade_date, 'energy_stress_score', energy_stress_score, payload)
   312	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date, metric_key) DO UPDATE
   313	    SET metric_value = EXCLUDED.metric_value,
   314	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   315	        ingested_at = now();
   316	  GET DIAGNOSTICS v_records_upserted = ROW_COUNT;
   317	
   318	  INSERT INTO analytics.driver_attribution_1d (trade_date, rank, factor, contribution, confidence, payload)
   319	  VALUES
   320	    (v_trade_date, 1, 'energy_transmission', energy_stress_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(energy_stress_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   321	    (v_trade_date, 2, 'macro_policy_uncertainty', tariff_threat_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(tariff_threat_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   322	    (v_trade_date, 3, 'china_flow_currency', china_tension_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(china_tension_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   323	    (v_trade_date, 4, 'crush_margin_oil_share', crush_pressure_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(crush_pressure_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   324	    (v_trade_date, 5, 'vix_volatility_regime', vix_stress_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(vix_stress_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload)
   325	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date, rank) DO UPDATE
   326	    SET factor = EXCLUDED.factor,
   327	        contribution = EXCLUDED.contribution,
   328	        confidence = EXCLUDED.confidence,
   329	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   330	        ingested_at = now();
   331	
   332	  INSERT INTO analytics.market_posture (trade_date, posture, rationale, payload)
   333	  VALUES (
   334	    v_trade_date,
   335	    posture,
   336	    format(
   337	      'Buyer posture %s from average score %s; top channel %s at %s.',
   338	      posture,
   339	      to_char(avg_score, 'FM999990.0'),
   340	      top_driver_key,
   341	      to_char(top_driver_score, 'FM999990.0')
   342	    ),
   343	    jsonb_build_object('averageScore', avg_score, 'topDriver', top_driver_key, 'topDriverScore', top_driver_score, 'asOf', now_et_iso, 'source', 'supabase_pg_cron_trusted_fill')
   344	  )
   345	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date) DO UPDATE
   346	    SET posture = EXCLUDED.posture,
   347	        rationale = EXCLUDED.rationale,
   348	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   349	        ingested_at = now();
   350	
   351	  INSERT INTO analytics.regime_state_1d (trade_date, regime, confidence, payload)
   352	  VALUES (
   353	    v_trade_date,
   354	    regime,
   355	    regime_confidence,
   356	    jsonb_build_object('averageScore', avg_score, 'asOf', now_et_iso, 'source', 'supabase_pg_cron_trusted_fill')
   357	  )
   358	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date) DO UPDATE
   359	    SET regime = EXCLUDED.regime,
   360	        confidence = EXCLUDED.confidence,
   361	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   362	        ingested_at = now();
   363	
   364	  UPDATE ops.ingest_run
   365	  SET status = 'ok',
   366	      finished_at = now(),
   367	      records_upserted = v_records_upserted,
   368	      error_message = NULL,
   369	      ingested_at = now()
   370	  WHERE run_id = v_run_id;
   371	
   372	  RETURN jsonb_build_object(
   373	    'status', 'ok',
   374	    'tradeDate', v_trade_date,
   375	    'recordsUpserted', v_records_upserted,
   376	    'topDriver', top_driver_key,
   377	    'topScore', top_driver_score,
   378	    'averageScore', avg_score
   379	  );
   380	EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
   381	  UPDATE ops.ingest_run
   382	  SET status = 'error',
   383	      finished_at = now(),
   384	      error_message = left(SQLERRM, 1000),
   385	      ingested_at = now()
   386	  WHERE run_id = v_run_id;
   387	  RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'error', 'message', SQLERRM);
   388	END;
   389	$$;
   390	
   391	DO $$
   392	DECLARE
   393	  job_id BIGINT;
   394	BEGIN
   395	  FOR job_id IN
   396	    SELECT jobid
   397	    FROM cron.job
   398	    WHERE jobname = 'trusted_site_fill'
   399	       OR command ILIKE '%ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill(%'
   400	  LOOP
   401	    PERFORM cron.unschedule(job_id);
   402	  END LOOP;
   403	END
   404	$$;

   406	-- Hourly refresh at :17 to keep dashboard drivers fresh without high-frequency pull cost.

   409	  '17 * * * *',
   410	  $$SELECT ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill()$$

     1	import { createServerClient } from "@supabase/ssr";

     4	
     5	function isPublicPath(pathname: string): boolean {
     6	  // Landing page
     7	  if (pathname === "/") return true;
     8	  // All auth flows (login, sign-up, callback, confirm, error, etc.)
     9	  if (pathname.startsWith("/auth/")) return true;
    10	  // Public health check endpoint for uptime monitoring
    11	  if (pathname === "/api/health") return true;
    12	  return false;
    13	}
    14	
    15	function isCronPath(pathname: string): boolean {
    16	  return pathname.startsWith("/api/cron/");
    17	}
    18	
    19	function buildLoginRedirect(request: NextRequest): NextResponse {
    20	  const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
    21	  const next = `${request.nextUrl.pathname}${request.nextUrl.search}`;
    22	  url.pathname = "/auth/login";
    23	  url.searchParams.set("next", next);
    24	  return NextResponse.redirect(url);
    25	}
    26	
    27	export async function updateSession(request: NextRequest) {
    28	  const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;
    29	
    30	  let supabaseResponse = NextResponse.next({
    31	    request,
    32	  });
    33	
    34	  // Public splash and auth flows remain reachable without a session.
    35	  if (isPublicPath(pathname)) {
    36	    return supabaseResponse;
    37	  }
    38	
    39	  // Cron routes are machine-to-machine; they enforce CRON_SECRET per route.
    40	  if (isCronPath(pathname)) {
    41	    return supabaseResponse;
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  // Fail closed if auth env is missing for protected surfaces.
    45	  if (!hasEnvVars) {
    46	    if (pathname.startsWith("/api/")) {
    47	      return NextResponse.json(
    48	        { ok: false, error: "Supabase auth env vars are not configured" },
    49	        { status: 503 },
    50	      );
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    return buildLoginRedirect(request);
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  // With Fluid compute, don't put this client in a global environment
    57	  // variable. Always create a new one on each request.
    58	  const supabase = createServerClient(
    59	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    60	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY!,
    61	    {
    62	      cookies: {
    63	        getAll() {
    64	          return request.cookies.getAll();
    65	        },
    66	        setAll(cookiesToSet) {
    67	          cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value }) =>
    68	            request.cookies.set(name, value),
    69	          );
    70	          supabaseResponse = NextResponse.next({
    71	            request,
    72	          });
    73	          cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>
    74	            supabaseResponse.cookies.set(name, value, options),
    75	          );
    76	        },
    77	      },
    78	    },
    79	  );
    80	
    81	  // Do not run code between createServerClient and
    82	  // supabase.auth.getClaims(). A simple mistake could make it very hard to debug
    83	  // issues with users being randomly logged out.
    84	
    85	  // IMPORTANT: If you remove getClaims() and you use server-side rendering
    86	  // with the Supabase client, your users may be randomly logged out.
    87	  const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.getClaims();
    88	  const user = data?.claims;
    89	
    90	  if (error || !user) {
    91	    if (pathname.startsWith("/api/")) {
    92	      return NextResponse.json(
    93	        { ok: false, error: "Authentication required" },
    94	        { status: 401 },
    95	      );
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    return buildLoginRedirect(request);
    99	  }
   100	
   101	  // IMPORTANT: You *must* return the supabaseResponse object as it is.
   102	  // If you're creating a new response object with NextResponse.next() make sure to:
   103	  // 1. Pass the request in it, like so:
   104	  //    const myNewResponse = NextResponse.next({ request })
   105	  // 2. Copy over the cookies, like so:
   106	  //    myNewResponse.cookies.setAll(supabaseResponse.cookies.getAll())
   107	  // 3. Change the myNewResponse object to fit your needs, but avoid changing
   108	  //    the cookies!
   109	  // 4. Finally:
   110	  //    return myNewResponse
   111	  // If this is not done, you may be causing the browser and server to go out
   112	  // of sync and terminate the user's session prematurely!
   113	
   114	  return supabaseResponse;
   115	}

    15	  model_version: string | null;

    14	  horizon_days: number;
    15	  model_version: string | null;

    23	  return null;
    24	}

     5	type ForecastTarget = {
     6	  id: string;
     7	  horizonDays: number;
     8	  horizonLabel: string;
     9	  priceLow: number;
    10	  priceHigh: number;
    11	  oofPrice: number;
    12	  coveragePct: number | null;
    13	};
    14	
    15	const AG_HORIZON_DAYS = [30, 90, 180] as const;
    16	const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP: Record<number, (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number]> = {
    17	  7: 30,
    18	  14: 90,
    19	  30: 180,
    20	};
    21	
    22	function normalizeHorizon(row: {
    23	  horizon_days: number;
    24	  model_version: string | null;
    25	}): number | null {
    26	  if (AG_HORIZON_DAYS.includes(row.horizon_days as (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number])) {
    27	    return row.horizon_days;
    28	  }
    29	  if (row.model_version?.startsWith("trusted-fill-v1")) {
    30	    return LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP[row.horizon_days] ?? null;
    31	  }
    32	  return null;
    33	}
    34	
    35	function horizonLabel(days: number): string {
    36	  if (days === 30) return "1M";
    37	  if (days === 90) return "3M";
    38	  if (days === 180) return "6M";
    39	  return `${days}d`;
    40	}
    41	
    42	export async function GET() {
    43	  try {
    44	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
    45	
    46	    const { data: rows, error } = await supabase
    47	      .schema("forecasts")
    48	      .from("target_zones")
    49	      .select("forecast_date, horizon_days, p30, p50, p70, model_version")
    50	      .order("forecast_date", { ascending: false })
    51	      .limit(60);
    52	
    53	    if (error) {
    54	      return NextResponse.json(
    55	        { error: error.message, asOfDate: null, targets: [] as ForecastTarget[] },
    56	        { status: 500 },
    57	      );
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    if (!rows || rows.length === 0) {
    61	      return NextResponse.json({
    62	        asOfDate: null,
    63	        targets: [] as ForecastTarget[],
    64	      });
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    const asOfDate = rows[0].forecast_date;
    68	    const latestRows = rows.filter((r) => r.forecast_date === asOfDate);
    69	    const deduped = new Map<number, ForecastTarget>();
    70	    for (const row of latestRows) {
    71	      const horizonDays = normalizeHorizon(row);
    72	      if (!horizonDays) continue;
    73	      if (deduped.has(horizonDays)) continue;
    74	      deduped.set(horizonDays, {
    75	        id: `${row.forecast_date}-${horizonDays}`,
    76	        horizonDays,
    77	        horizonLabel: horizonLabel(horizonDays),
    78	        priceLow: Number(row.p30),
    79	        priceHigh: Number(row.p70),
    80	        oofPrice: Number(row.p50),
    81	        coveragePct: null,
    82	      });
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    const targets: ForecastTarget[] = [...deduped.values()]
    86	      .sort((a, b) => a.horizonDays - b.horizonDays)
    87	      .map((r) => ({
    88	        id: r.id,
    89	        horizonDays: r.horizonDays,
    90	        horizonLabel: r.horizonLabel,
    91	        priceLow: r.priceLow,
    92	        priceHigh: r.priceHigh,
    93	        oofPrice: r.oofPrice,
    94	        coveragePct: r.coveragePct,
    95	      }));
    96	
    97	    return NextResponse.json({
    98	      asOfDate,
    99	      targets,
   100	    });
   101	  } catch (err) {
   102	    return NextResponse.json(
   103	      { error: String(err), asOfDate: null, targets: [] as ForecastTarget[] },
   104	      { status: 500 },
   105	    );
   106	  }
   107	}

     1	import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
     2	
     3	import { createSupabaseAdminClient } from "@/lib/server/supabase-admin";
     4	import type { ApiEnvelope, ZlPriceBar } from "@/lib/contracts/api";
     5	
     6	type PriceRow = {
     7	  symbol: string;
     8	  bucket_ts: string;
     9	  open: number | string;
    10	  high: number | string;
    11	  low: number | string;
    12	  close: number | string;
    13	  volume: number | string | null;
    14	};
    15	
    16	function dayKey(tsIso: string): string {
    17	  return tsIso.slice(0, 10);
    18	}
    19	
    20	function buildLatestDatabentoDailyFromHourly(rows: PriceRow[]): ZlPriceBar | null {
    21	  if (rows.length === 0) return null;
    22	
    23	  const latestDay = dayKey(rows[0].bucket_ts);
    24	  const sameDayRows = rows.filter((row) => dayKey(row.bucket_ts) === latestDay);
    25	  if (sameDayRows.length === 0) return null;
    26	
    27	  sameDayRows.sort(
    28	    (a, b) => new Date(a.bucket_ts).getTime() - new Date(b.bucket_ts).getTime(),
    29	  );
    30	
    31	  const parsedRows = sameDayRows
    32	    .map((row) => ({
    33	      open: Number(row.open),
    34	      high: Number(row.high),
    35	      low: Number(row.low),
    36	      close: Number(row.close),
    37	      volume: Number(row.volume ?? 0),
    38	    }))
    39	    .filter(
    40	      (row) =>
    41	        Number.isFinite(row.open) &&
    42	        Number.isFinite(row.high) &&
    43	        Number.isFinite(row.low) &&
    44	        Number.isFinite(row.close),
    45	    );
    46	
    47	  if (parsedRows.length === 0) return null;
    48	
    49	  const open = parsedRows[0].open;
    50	  const close = parsedRows[parsedRows.length - 1].close;
    51	  let high = parsedRows[0].high;
    52	  let low = parsedRows[0].low;
    53	  let volume = 0;
    54	
    55	  for (const row of parsedRows) {
    56	    if (row.high > high) high = row.high;
    57	    if (row.low < low) low = row.low;
    58	    if (Number.isFinite(row.volume)) volume += row.volume;
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  return {
    62	    symbol: "ZL",
    63	    tradeDate: `${latestDay}T00:00:00+00:00`,
    64	    open,
    65	    high,
    66	    low,
    67	    close,
    68	    volume,
    69	  };
    70	}
    71	
    72	export async function GET() {
    73	  try {
    74	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
    75	
    76	    // Supabase Data API commonly enforces a max-row cap (default 1000).
    77	    // Pull newest rows first so we always include the current chart window.
    78	    const { data: rows, error } = await supabase
    79	      .schema("mkt")
    80	      .from("price_1d")
    81	      .select("symbol, bucket_ts, open, high, low, close, volume")
    82	      .eq("symbol", "ZL")
    83	      .order("bucket_ts", { ascending: false })
    84	      .limit(1000);
    85	
    86	    if (error) {
    87	      return NextResponse.json(
    88	        { ok: false, data: [], asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: error.message },
    89	        { status: 500 },
    90	      );
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    const bars: ZlPriceBar[] = (rows ?? [])
    94	      .map((row) => ({
    95	      symbol: row.symbol,
    96	      tradeDate: row.bucket_ts,
    97	      open: Number(row.open),
    98	      high: Number(row.high),
    99	      low: Number(row.low),
   100	      close: Number(row.close),
   101	      volume: Number(row.volume),
   102	      }))
   103	      .sort(
   104	        (a, b) => new Date(a.tradeDate).getTime() - new Date(b.tradeDate).getTime(),
   105	      );
   106	
   107	    const { data: hourlyRows } = await supabase
   108	      .schema("mkt")
   109	      .from("price_1h")
   110	      .select("symbol, bucket_ts, open, high, low, close, volume")
   111	      .eq("symbol", "ZL")
   112	      .order("bucket_ts", { ascending: false })
   113	      .limit(96);
   114	
   115	    const databentoLatest = buildLatestDatabentoDailyFromHourly(
   116	      (hourlyRows ?? []) as PriceRow[],
   117	    );
   118	
   119	    if (databentoLatest) {
   120	      const lastBar = bars[bars.length - 1] ?? null;
   121	      const lastDay = lastBar ? dayKey(lastBar.tradeDate) : null;
   122	      const databentoDay = dayKey(databentoLatest.tradeDate);
   123	
   124	      if (!lastDay || databentoDay > lastDay) {
   125	        bars.push(databentoLatest);
   126	      } else if (databentoDay === lastDay && lastBar) {
   127	        bars[bars.length - 1] = databentoLatest;
   128	      }
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    const envelope: ApiEnvelope<ZlPriceBar[]> = {
   132	      ok: true,
   133	      data: bars,
   134	      asOf: new Date().toISOString(),
   135	      source: databentoLatest
   136	        ? "mkt.price_1d + Databento (mkt.price_1h latest daily bar)"
   137	        : "mkt.price_1d",
   138	    };
   139	
   140	    return NextResponse.json(envelope);
   141	  } catch (err) {
   142	    return NextResponse.json(
   143	      { ok: false, data: [], asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: String(err) },
   144	      { status: 500 },
   145	    );
   146	  }
   147	}

    96	function toNumber(value: unknown): number | null {
    97	  if (value === null || value === undefined) return null;
    98	  const n = Number(value);
    99	  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : null;
   100	}
   101	
   102	function normalizeMetricKey(key: string): string {
   103	  return key.trim().toLowerCase();
   104	}
   105	
   106	function coerceScore(value: number | null): number | null {
   107	  if (value === null) return null;
   108	  const abs = Math.abs(value);
   109	  if (abs <= 1) return Math.round(abs * 1000) / 10;
   110	  if (abs <= 100) return Math.round(abs * 10) / 10;
   111	  return 100;
   112	}
   113	
   114	function mapFactorToDriver(factor: string): DriverKey | null {
   115	  const f = factor.toLowerCase();
   116	  if (f.includes("vix") || f.includes("volatility")) return "vix_stress";
   117	  if (f.includes("crush")) return "crush_pressure";
   118	  if (f.includes("china") || f.includes("cny")) return "china_tension";
   119	  if (f.includes("tariff") || f.includes("policy") || f.includes("tpu") || f.includes("emv")) return "tariff_threat";
   120	  if (f.includes("energy") || f.includes("crude") || f.includes("oil") || f.includes("cl")) return "energy_stress";
   121	  return null;
   122	}
   123	
   124	function levelFor(driver: DriverKey, score: number | null): string {
   125	  if (score === null) return "No Data";
   126	
   127	  if (driver === "vix_stress") {
   128	    if (score >= 85) return "Gap Risk";
   129	    if (score >= 65) return "Fund Exit";
   130	    if (score >= 45) return "Elevated";
   131	    return "Calm";
   132	  }
   133	  if (driver === "crush_pressure") {
   134	    if (score >= 85) return "Plant Idling";
   135	    if (score >= 65) return "Margin Squeeze";
   136	    if (score >= 45) return "Breakeven Risk";
   137	    return "Strong";
   138	  }
   139	  if (driver === "china_tension") {
   140	    if (score >= 80) return "Active Conflict";
   141	    if (score >= 60) return "Trade Diversion";
   142	    if (score >= 40) return "Monitor Flows";
   143	    return "Brazil Favored";
   144	  }
   145	  if (driver === "tariff_threat") {
   146	    if (score >= 85) return "Systemic Shock";
   147	    if (score >= 65) return "Elevated Risk";
   148	    if (score >= 45) return "Watch";
   149	    return "Contained";
   150	  }
   151	  if (score >= 85) return "Crisis";
   152	  if (score >= 65) return "Supply Shock";
   153	  if (score >= 45) return "Elevated";
   154	  return "Low Risk";
   155	}
   156	
   157	function regimeFor(score: number | null): string {
   158	  if (score === null) return "NO_DATA";
   159	  if (score >= 70) return "PRESSURE";
   160	  if (score >= 45) return "WATCH";
   161	  return "CALM";
   162	}
   163	
   164	function outlookFromScore(score: number): "BULLISH" | "NEUTRAL" | "CAUTIOUS" | "BEARISH" {
   165	  if (score >= 70) return "BEARISH";
   166	  if (score >= 55) return "CAUTIOUS";
   167	  if (score >= 35) return "NEUTRAL";
   168	  return "BULLISH";
   169	}

    60	function formatFreshnessLabel(
    61	  payload: Pick<MarketDriversResponse, "as_of_date" | "as_of_date_min" | "as_of_date_max" | "mixed_vintage"> | null | undefined,
    62	): string | null {
    63	  if (!payload) return null
    64	  if (payload.mixed_vintage && payload.as_of_date_min && payload.as_of_date_max) {
    65	    return `Mixed vintage ${payload.as_of_date_min} to ${payload.as_of_date_max}`
    66	  }
    67	  return payload.as_of_date ? `Data as of ${payload.as_of_date}` : null
    68	}
    69	
    70	function formatFreshnessSummary(
    71	  payload: Pick<MarketDriversResponse, "as_of_date" | "as_of_date_min" | "as_of_date_max" | "mixed_vintage"> | null | undefined,
    72	): string {
    73	  if (!payload) return "–"
    74	  if (payload.mixed_vintage && payload.as_of_date_min && payload.as_of_date_max) {
    75	    return `${payload.as_of_date_min} to ${payload.as_of_date_max}`
    76	  }
    77	  return payload.as_of_date ?? "–"
    78	}

   118	function getScoreColor(score: number): { stroke: string; glow: string } {
   119	  const s = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, score))
   120	  if (s <= 25) return { stroke: "#22C55E", glow: "rgba(34,197,94,0.5)" }
   121	  if (s <= 40) {
   122	    const t = (s - 25) / 15
   123	    return {
   124	      stroke: `rgb(${Math.round(34 + (234 - 34) * t)}, ${Math.round(197 - (197 - 179) * t)}, ${Math.round(94 - (94 - 8) * t)})`,
   125	      glow: `rgba(${Math.round(34 + (234 - 34) * t)}, ${Math.round(197 - (197 - 179) * t)}, ${Math.round(94 - (94 - 8) * t)}, 0.5)`,
   126	    }
   127	  }
   128	  if (s <= 55) return { stroke: "#EAB308", glow: "rgba(234,179,8,0.5)" }
   129	  if (s <= 70) {
   130	    const t = (s - 55) / 15
   131	    return {
   132	      stroke: `rgb(${Math.round(234 + (239 - 234) * t)}, ${Math.round(179 - (179 - 115) * t)}, ${Math.round(8 + (0 - 8) * t)})`,
   133	      glow: `rgba(${Math.round(234 + (239 - 234) * t)}, ${Math.round(179 - (179 - 115) * t)}, ${Math.round(8 + (0 - 8) * t)}, 0.5)`,
   134	    }
   135	  }
   136	  if (s <= 85) return { stroke: "#EF7300", glow: "rgba(239,115,0,0.5)" }
   137	  return { stroke: "#EF4444", glow: "rgba(239,68,68,0.6)" }
   138	}

     7	  reasoningEffort: string;
     8	  source?: string;

    13	  enabled: boolean;
    14	  source: string;
    15	  model: string | null;
    16	  reasoningEffort: string | null;
    17	  generatedAt: string | null;
    18	  refreshScheduleEt: string | null;
    19	};

    21	const TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES = new Set([
    22	  "trusted-live-pull",
    23	  "trusted-authority-pull",
    24	  "ai-daily-refresh",
    25	  "chatgpt-pro-subscription-refresh",
    26	]);
    27	
    28	const SNAPSHOT_LOADERS: Record<string, () => Promise<unknown>> = {
    29	  "app/config/dashboard-risk-factors-ai.json": async () =>
    30	    (await import("@/app/config/dashboard-risk-factors-ai.json")).default,
    31	  "app/config/strategy-posture-ai.json": async () =>
    32	    (await import("@/app/config/strategy-posture-ai.json")).default,
    33	  "app/config/sentiment-overview-ai.json": async () =>
    34	    (await import("@/app/config/sentiment-overview-ai.json")).default,
    35	  "app/config/legislation-feed-ai.json": async () =>
    36	    (await import("@/app/config/legislation-feed-ai.json")).default,
    37	  "app/config/vegas-intel-ai.json": async () =>
    38	    (await import("@/app/config/vegas-intel-ai.json")).default,
    39	};
    40	
    41	function coerceSnapshot<T extends object>(parsed: unknown): (T & AiSnapshotMeta) | null {
    42	  if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== "object") return null;
    43	  const candidate = parsed as T & Partial<AiSnapshotMeta>;
    44	  if (typeof candidate.generatedAt !== "string" || candidate.generatedAt.trim().length === 0) return null;
    45	  if (typeof candidate.model !== "string" || candidate.model.trim().length === 0) return null;
    46	  if (typeof candidate.reasoningEffort !== "string" || candidate.reasoningEffort.trim().length === 0) return null;
    47	  const snapshotSource =
    48	    typeof candidate.source === "string" ? candidate.source.trim().toLowerCase() : "";
    49	  if (!TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES.has(snapshotSource)) return null;
    50	  return candidate as T & AiSnapshotMeta;
    51	}
    52	
    53	export async function readAiSnapshot<T extends object>(
    54	  relativePathFromRepoRoot: string,
    55	): Promise<(T & AiSnapshotMeta) | null> {
    56	  try {
    57	    const loader = SNAPSHOT_LOADERS[relativePathFromRepoRoot];
    58	    if (loader) {
    59	      const imported = await loader();
    60	      const validated = coerceSnapshot<T>(imported);
    61	      if (validated) return validated;
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    const fullPath = path.join(
    65	      /* turbopackIgnore: true */ process.cwd(),
    66	      relativePathFromRepoRoot,
    67	    );
    68	    const raw = await readFile(fullPath, "utf8");
    69	    return coerceSnapshot<T>(JSON.parse(raw));
    70	  } catch {
    71	    return null;
    72	  }
    73	}
    74	
    75	export function toAiEnvelopeMeta(snapshot: AiSnapshotMeta | null): AiEnvelopeMeta {
    76	  return {
    77	    enabled: Boolean(snapshot),
    78	    source: snapshot?.source ?? "none",
    79	    model: snapshot?.model ?? null,
    80	    reasoningEffort: snapshot?.reasoningEffort ?? null,
    81	    generatedAt: snapshot?.generatedAt ?? null,
    82	    refreshScheduleEt: snapshot?.refreshScheduleEt ?? null,
    83	  };
    84	}

    12	check_snapshot() {
    13	  local generated="$1"
    14	  local baseline="$2"
    15	  if diff -u "$baseline" "$generated" >/dev/null; then
    16	    echo "PASS  $(basename "$baseline")"
    17	  else
    18	    echo "FAIL  $(basename "$baseline")"
    19	    diff -u "$baseline" "$generated"
    20	    return 1
    21	  fi
    22	}
